moxdisgan pirobiT vadamde ganTavisuflebis sakiTxis dadebiTad ga-


daawyvetad. sasjelaRsrulebis dawesebulebis administracia axasi-


aTebs dadebiTad. kerZod, daxasiaTebaSi miTiTebulia, rom v. Jidko-


vi inaniebs Cadenil danaSauls; masze dakisrebul movaleobebs asru-


lebs keTilsindisierad; sasjelis moxdis periodSi reJimis moTxov-


naTa darRvevaSi SemCneuli ar yofila; SeniSvnebze gagebiT reagi-


rebs; administraciis mier waxalisebulia erTxel _ gamocxadebuli


aqvs madlobebi, aris 67 wlisa.


zemoaRniSnulis gaTvaliswinebiT, palatas miaqnia, rom msjavrde-


bul v. Jidkovis gamosworebisaTvis saWiro ar aris daniSnuli sasje-


lis mTlianad moxda da mizanSewonilad Tvlis, v. Jidkovi pirobiT


vadamde gaTavisufldes darCenili sasjelis moxdisagan.

g. borCxaZe (Tavmjdomare),


m. gogelia, 


m. isaevi


ganixila advokat p. gogalaZis kerZo sakasacio saCivari mcxeTis


raionuli sasamarTlos mosamarTlis 2004w. 25 agvistos brZanebaze,


romliTac dakmayofilda mcxeTa-mTianeTis saolqo prokuraturis


Suamdgomloba mcxeTis raionis sof. diRomSi mdebare a. zukakiSvi-


lis saxelze ricxul 11300 kv. metri farTobis mqone sam miwis nakveT-


ze yadaRis dadebis Sesaxeb.


aRwerilobiTi nawili:


mcxeTa-mTianeTis saolqo prokuraturis warmoebaSi arsebuli


sisxlis samarTlis saqmis mixedviT, n. lasuraSvili iyo ra sof. diR-


mis miwis reformis komisiis Tavmjdomare, Tanamdeboba gamoiyena bo-


rotad da imave komisiis wevrs _ a. zukakiSvils 1992w. 5 oqtombris


dadgenilebiT ukanonod gamouyo sami miwis nakveTi, romelTa saerTo


farTobi erT heqtarsa da 1300 kv. metrs Seadgens. 


zemoaRniSnul miwis nakveTebze yadaRis dadeba prokuraturam


iSuamdgomla im motiviT, rom saqmeze saboloo gadawyvetilebis mi-


Rebamde ar moxdes maTi gasxviseba.


kerZo sakasacio saCivari miiCnevs, rom sasamarTlom prokuratu-


ris Suamdgomloba ganixila saproceso kanonmdeblobis darRveviT


da gamosca ukanono brZaneba.


palatis sxdomaze advokatma p. gogalaZem iTxova gasaCivrebuli


brZanebis gauqmeba da prokuraturis Suamdgomlobis xelaxla gansa-


xilvelad sxva mosamarTlisaTvis gadacema.


prokurorma T. oTinaSvilma mxari ar dauWira advokatis moTxov-


nas da iSuamdgomla gasaCivrebuli brZanebis ucvlelad datoveba.


samotivacio nawili:


palatam mousmina mxareebs, Seiswavla saqmis masalebi, gaaanaliza


saCivris safuZvlianoba da mivida im daskvnamde, rom mosamarTlis


1881


brZaneba unda gauqmdes da prokuraturis Suamdgomloba xelaxali


ganxilvisaTvis gadaeces imave sasamarTlos sxva mosamarTles Semde-

nebaze yadaRis dadebis Sesaxeb Suamdgomlobas mosamarTle ganixi-

da im organos warmomadgenlis monawileobiT, romelmac Suamdgom-


lobiT mimarTa sasamarTlos. sasamarTlo sxdomaSi monawileobis


ufleba aqvs braldebuls (aseve im pirs, visi qonebis dayadaRebazec


aRZrulia Suamdgomloba), agreTve maT damcvelebsa da kanonier war-


momadgenlebs. mocemul konkretul SemTxvevaSi mosamarTlem ise ga-


nixila prokuraturis Suamdgomloba, rom amis Taobaze arc bralde-


bul n. lasuraSvils Seatyobina da arc _ miwis mesakuTre a. zukakiS-


vils. amiT sasamarTlom daarRvia sssk-is me-15 muxliT dawesebuli


SejibrebiTobis principi, saxeldobr: aRniSnuli muxlis mesame nawi-


liT dadgenilia, rom: `mxareebs sruli Tanasworobis safuZvelze


ufleba aqvT, waradginon mtkicebulebani, monawileoba miiRon maT


gamokvlevaSi, ganacxadon Suamdgomloba da acileba, gamoTqvan saku-


Tari azri sisxlis samarTlis saqmis nebismier sakiTxze”. am darRve-


vam gamoiwvia procesSi monawileobis uflebamosilebis mqone pirTa


uflebebis SezRudva, rac saproceso kanonis arsebiT darRvevas da


sasamarTlos mier miRebuli gadawyvetilebis gauqmebis udavo sa-


fuZvels warmoadgens.

571-e muxlebiT,
